Conclusion: 高性能嵌入模型并非以任意方式组织语义空间，而是表现出可度量的一致结构特征。该发现加深了对嵌入空间结构与模型性能关系的理解，并提示未来可设计更有针对性的训练目标或优化条件嵌入方法。

Abstract: In this paper, we show that high-performing embedding models organize their embedding spaces in a consistent way. We evaluate 25 contemporary embedding models on five MTEB tasks spanning four diverse task categories (retrieval, bitext mining, pair classification, and summarization) in both English and multilingual settings, and reveal that nearest-neighbor overlap and magnitude differences in independent component analysis (ICA) between paired text instances strongly correlate (even up to 0.97) with performance on the given task. Ultimately, we show that embedding tasks display varying degrees of linearity and reliance on retention of local information. Our results further the understanding of embeddings, their relation to model performance, and shed light on possible future training objectives and optimizing conditional embeddings.

### [148] [GHI: Graphormer over Conditioned Hypergraph Incidence for Aspect-Based Sentiment Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22228)
*Yu Du,Wenlong Zhu,Xingze Li,Chenglong Cao,Jing Wang,Yukun Ma*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ABSA 需要模型将情感证据准确绑定到对应方面词，是检验细粒度结构推理能力的典型任务。现有大规模模型虽有效，但参数规模大；传统模型在复杂或鲁棒性场景下容易退化，因此需要一种紧凑且结构感知的替代方案。

Method: 作者提出 GHI，将语言和语义证据表示为 token--hyperedge 的关联关系，并在条件化超图关联结构上使用 Graphormer 进行推理。该方法通过统一的 incidence 接口融合多种结构信号，并基于二部图拓扑构建结构推理层。

Result: 在六个标准 ABSA 基准上，GHI 在 SemEval 领域优于所有基线；多随机种子实验显示其相较强 DeBERTa 基线具有稳定提升。仅用 247M 参数，GHI 在 ISE benchmark 上接近 11B Flan-T5 方法表现；在 ARTS 数据集上也展现出较强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 结果表明，对于 ABSA 等细粒度任务，紧凑的结构推理模型仍然是规模驱动大模型之外的有价值替代路线，尤其在方面—证据绑定与鲁棒性方面具有优势。

Abstract: Aspect-based sentiment analysis (ABSA) requires models to bind sentiment evidence to the correct aspect, making it a natural testbed for fine-grained structural reasoning. We introduce GHI, a Graphormer-over-Conditioned-Hypergraph-Incidence framework that is designed as an incidence-based structural reasoning layer built on a bipartite topology. GHI represents diverse linguistic and semantic evidence as token--hyperedge incidence relations, allowing different structural signals to be incorporated through a unified interface. Extensive experiments on six standard ABSA benchmarks show that GHI outperforms all baselines on the SemEval domains, and multi-seed evaluations show stable improvements over strong DeBERTa. Further experiments show that with only 247M parameters, GHI approaches the performance of 11B Flan-T5 based methods on the ISE benchmark. Moreover, it demonstrates strong robustness on the challenging ARTS datasets, maintaining highly competitive performance where traditional models degrade. These results demonstrate that compact structural reasoning remains a valuable alternative to scale-driven approaches for fine-grained tasks.

*Kai Golan Hashiloni,Daniel Fadlon,Lior Livyatan,Ofri Hefetz,Jiahuan Pei,Kfir Bar*

TL;DR: 本文提出 IdioLink，一个用于评测模型能否将习语表达与字面或改写形式中的等价概念意义相链接的检索基准。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 习语的意义通常无法仅从表层词形推断，需要模型具备超越词汇重合的语义抽象能力；现有检索模型是否真正理解习语意义仍缺乏针对性评测。

Method: 构建包含 10,700 篇文档、2,140 个查询、覆盖 107 个习语的基准数据集，涵盖习语的字面用法与比喻用法，并为查询和文档标注表达核心意义的文本片段；使用 BGE、E5、Contriever、Qwen 等强嵌入模型进行检索评测。

Result: 实验表明，当前强基线模型在跨表层差异表达检索等价意义时表现不足，往往依赖主题相关性和浅层语义线索，而非真正的习语语义理解。

Conclusion: IdioLink 揭示了现有语义检索模型在习语理解与语义抽象方面的关键缺口，可作为未来习语感知检索模型的重要评测平台。

Abstract: Idioms pose a fundamental challenge for language models, as their meaning cannot be inferred from surface form alone. Understanding such expressions, therefore, requires semantic abstraction beyond lexical overlap. We introduce IdioLink, a retrieval benchmark designed to test whether models can link idiomatic expressions to conceptually equivalent meanings expressed in literal or paraphrased forms. IdioLink comprises 10,700 documents and 2,140 queries, spanning 107 idioms with both literal and figurative uses. Each document and query is annotated with spans that convey the core meaning. Evaluating strong embedding baselines (e.g., BGE, E5, Contriever, and Qwen), we show that current models struggle to retrieve equivalent meanings across divergent surface realizations, relying instead on topical and shallow semantic cues. IdioLink exposes key gaps in idiom-aware semantic retrieval and provides a challenging testbed for future models.

### [150] [Harder to Defend: Towards Chinese Toxicity Attacks via Implicit Enhancement and Obfuscation Rewriting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22258)
*Jingyi Kang,Junyu Lu,Bo Xu,Hongbo Wang,Linlin zong,Roy Ka-Wei Lee,Hongfei Lin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型有害性评估多关注显式表述，而中文场景中有害意图常通过语义间接表达与表面混淆共同呈现，导致检测器漏检风险较高，相关系统化评测不足。

Method: 作者构建 Chinese Implicit Toxicity Attack（CITA）框架，包含三个阶段：有害意图学习、隐式有害性增强、混淆变体重写。该框架旨在保持原始有害意图、增强表达隐晦性，并生成受控表面变体。同时，利用 CITA 生成的红队数据微调 Chinese Implicit Toxicity Defense（CITD）模型。

Result: 在 CITA 生成的评测样本上，七个被测试检测器表现出显著漏检风险，平均攻击成功率（ASR）达到 69.48%。人工评估确认样本保留了有害性，同时提升了隐式性与规避性。使用 CITA 数据训练的 CITD 在鲁棒性方面有所提升。

Conclusion: 论文表明，中文隐式有害内容检测仍存在明显薄弱环节；受控红队数据不仅可用于揭示检测器缺陷，也可作为防御训练数据提升模型鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) require robust toxicity evaluation beyond explicit wording. This setting remains underexplored in Chinese, where toxicity may combine semantic indirectness with surface obfuscation. We introduce Chinese Implicit Toxicity Attack (CITA), a controlled red-team evaluation and defense-data generation framework, not a deployable evasion tool. CITA uses three stages: (i) Harmful Intent Learning, (ii) Implicit Toxicity Enhancement, and (iii) Obfuscation Variant Rewriting, to preserve harmful intent, increase implicitness, and add controlled surface variants. On CITA-generated evaluation samples, the seven tested detectors exhibit substantial missed-detection risks, reaching an average ASR of 69.48%; human evaluation further confirms preserved harmfulness and increased implicitness/evasiveness. As a downstream defense application, we fine-tune a Chinese Implicit Toxicity Defense model (CITD) with CITA-generated red-team data, showing that such data can improve robustness through additional training.

### [151] [Pattern-and-root inflectional morphology: the Arabic broken plural](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22310)
*Alexis Amid Neme,Eric Laporte*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出并实现了一个阿拉伯语名词屈折形态描述模型，将传统“词根-模板”框架反转为“模板-词根”，并以词典化方式处理包括破碎复数在内的名词屈折。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿拉伯语名词形态复杂，尤其破碎复数涉及词干内部变化；传统分析常把屈折、派生、语义及音系/正字法规则混合处理，不利于由阿拉伯语语言学家维护词典和语言资源。论文旨在建立一种结构清晰、可更新、便于编码和实际分析的名词屈折资源模型。

Method: 模型基于传统词根与模板概念，但优先描述模板，再关联词根；将屈折形式描述与派生、语义分离。词典以全变音符号化的引理词条组织，形态分析直接依赖词形词典，不使用形态音系规则。作者简化单数模板分类，仅区分元音长短，不区分元音音质；将词根交替和正字法变体作为独立事实编码。

Result: 论文给出破碎复数名词的细粒度分类：三辅音破碎复数分为22个模板、90个类别；四辅音破碎复数分为3个模板、70个类别。若考虑只影响单数的屈折变体，总计形成300个屈折类别。该编码方案已应用于3200个破碎复数名词词条。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，以模板优先、词典驱动、规则最小化的方式描述阿拉伯语名词屈折是可行且实用的；其分类体系较为简洁、有序并适合资源维护，尤其适用于破碎复数的系统化编码和形态分析。

Abstract: We present a substantially implemented model of description of the inflectional morphology of Arabic nouns, with special attention to the management of dictionaries and other language resources by Arabic-speaking linguists. The breakthrough lies in the reversal of the traditional root-and-pattern Semitic model into pattern-and-root, giving precedence to patterns over roots. Our model includes broken plurals (BPs), i.e. plurals formed by modifying the stem. It is based on the traditional notions of root and pattern of Semitic morphology. However, as compared to traditional Arabic morphology, it keeps the formal description of inflection separate from that of derivation and semantics. As traditional Arabic dictionaries, the updatable dictionary is structured in lexical entries for lemmas, and the reference spelling is fully diacritized. In our model, morphological analysis of Arabic text is performed directly with a dictionary of words and without morphophonological rules. Our taxonomy for noun inflection is simple, orderly and detailed. We simplify the taxonomy of singular patterns by specifying vowel quantity as v or vv, and ignoring vowel quality. Root alternations and orthographical variations are encoded independently from patterns and in a factual way, without deep roots or morphophonological or orthographical rules. Nouns with a triliteral BP are classified according to 22 patterns subdivided into 90 classes, and nouns with a quadriliteral BP according to 3 patterns subdivided into 70 classes. These 160 classes become 300 inflectional classes when we take into account inflectional variations that affect only the singular. We provide a straightforward encoding scheme that we applied to 3 200 entries of BP nouns.

### [155] [Unified Data Selection for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22389)
*Xiaoyuan Li,Yubo Ma,Chengpeng Li,Fengbin Zhu,Yiyao Yu,Keqin Bao,Wenjie Wang,Fuli Feng,Dayiheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 High-Entropy Sum（HES），一种无需训练的推理样本质量评估指标，通过累加推理样本中最高熵少量 token 的熵值来筛选高质量长链式思维数据，并在 SFT、RFT、RL 三种训练范式中验证其有效性与高效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂长 CoT 推理能力训练依赖大量高质量推理数据；现有数据筛选或评估方法通常计算成本高，或难以稳定区分高质量与低质量推理样本，因此需要一种低成本、可靠、统一的数据质量度量。

Method: 提出训练无关指标 HES：对每个推理样本，仅选取熵最高的一小部分 token（如 0.5%），将其熵值求和作为样本质量分数。随后将 HES 用于 SFT 数据筛选、RFT 样本选择以及 RL 中成功轨迹筛选，并与基线方法进行比较。

Result: 在 SFT 中，仅使用 HES 排名前 20% 的数据即可达到全量数据训练效果，而使用低 HES 数据会降低性能；在 RFT 中，基于 HES 的训练显著优于基线方法；在 RL 中，HES 筛选出的成功轨迹帮助模型学习更强推理模式，并显著超过对比方法，同时降低计算开销。

Conclusion: HES 是一种鲁棒、训练免费且高效的推理质量度量，可作为统一的数据筛选机制，提升 LLM 在复杂长 CoT 推理任务中的训练效率与性能。

Abstract: Effectively training Large Language Models (LLMs) for complex, long-CoT reasoning is often bottlenecked by the need for massive high-quality reasoning data. Existing methods are either computationally expensive or fail to reliably distinguish high- from low-quality reasoning samples. To address this, we propose High-Entropy Sum (HES), a training-free metric that quantifies reasoning quality by summing only the entropy of the top (e.g., 0.5\%) highest-entropy tokens in each reasoning sample. We validate HES across three mainstream training paradigms: Supervised Fine-tuning (SFT), Rejection Fine-tuning (RFT), and Reinforcement Learning (RL), with extensive results demonstrating its consistent effectiveness and significantly reduced computational overhead. In SFT, training on the top 20\% HES-ranked data matches full-dataset performance, while using the lowest-HES data degrades it. In RFT, our HES-based training approach significantly outperforms baseline methods. In RL, HES-selected successful trajectories enable the model to learn strong reasoning patterns, significantly surpassing other compared methods. Our findings establish HES as a robust, training-free metric that enables a unified, effective, and efficient method for developing advanced reasoning in LLMs.

Abstract: The study of online discourse has become central to understanding societal polarization. While much research has focused on detecting overt toxicity, the subtle dynamics of social cohesion, meaning the interaction between divisive and unifying narratives, remain computationally underexplored (Bail, 2021; Gonzalez-Bailon and Lelkes, 2023). This paper presents Cohesion-6K, a manually and ChatGPT-assisted annotated dataset of six thousand Arabic public Facebook posts related to the Israeli Occupation of Palestine. Cohesion-6K provides a transparent and reproducible resource for the study of online cohesion and polarization. ### [158] [From Correlation to Cause: A Five-Stage Methodology for Feature Analysis in Transformer Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22462)
*Caleb Munigety*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出并演示了一个用于Transformer语言模型因果特征分析的五阶段流程，发现IOI任务中的电路具有较强可迁移性，但SAE提取的名称选择性特征只有部分因果作用，且部署监控在给定成本假设下可显著降低预期成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释性研究常能检测到模型内部特征或电路，但单独的检测结果不足以证明其因果作用、鲁棒性与实际部署价值。本文希望建立一个端到端方法，将探针设计、特征提取、因果验证、鲁棒性测试和部署评估连接起来。

Method: 作者在GPT-2 small的间接宾语识别（IOI）任务上实施五阶段方法：通过activation patching识别经典IOI电路；用稀疏自编码器提取名称选择性特征；通过特征消融进行因果验证；在三种分布偏移下测试检测与因果鲁棒性；最后用误报/漏报成本模型评估监控配置的部署收益。

Result: activation patching恢复了经典IOI电路，其中layer-9 head 9单独带来+1.02恢复；SAE得到每个名称选择性特征，效应大小约30到50激活单位；但消融15个特征后模型仍在98%的提示上保持正确。15个选择性特征仅解释31%的激活方差，而SAE整体解释99.7%；选择性比率与因果强度负相关（r=-0.56）。分布偏移下电路转移较好，但特征消融效应明显退化。成本评估中最优监控配置为每1000次查询成本8.96美元，相比1000美元基线节省99.1%。

Conclusion: 本文表明，特征可检测性不等同于强因果性或部署可靠性；只有将电路定位、特征提取、因果验证、鲁棒性和成本评估结合起来，才能获得更完整的机制解释和实际应用判断。

Abstract: We propose a five-stage methodology for causal feature analysis in transformer language models (probe design, feature extraction, causal validation, robustness testing, and deployment integration) and demonstrate it end-to-end on GPT-2 small performing the Indirect Object Identification (IOI) task. Activation patching recovers the canonical IOI circuit (layer-9 head 9 alone gives recovery +1.02). A sparse autoencoder recovers per-name selective features with effect sizes of 30 to 50 activation units. Causal validation finds these features specifically but only partially causal: ablating fifteen of them leaves the model accurate on 98% of prompts. Two NLA-inspired evaluations strengthen this picture: the fifteen selective features explain only 31% of activation variance versus the SAE's 99.7%, and selectivity ratio anticorrelates with causal force (r = -0.56). Robustness testing under three distribution shifts finds that the circuit transfers cleanly but feature ablation effects degrade substantially, exposing a gap between detection robustness and causal robustness. A cost-based deployment evaluation (assumed $50/FN, $0.42/FP, 2% error rate) finds an optimal monitor configuration yielding $8.96 per 1000 queries against a $1000 baseline, a 99.1% saving. Optimal composition strategy varies with cost ratio and base rate. The conjunction of stages produces findings no single stage would.

</details>

### [161] [Scene Abstraction for Lexical Semantics: Structured Representations of Situated Meaning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22542)
*Yejin Cho,Katrin Erk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 Scene Abstraction，用结构化方式表示词语在具体使用语境中参与的解释性场景，并构建数据集与实验验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统词义计算表示多关注词汇的抽象语义相似性，难以捕捉词语在真实使用中唤起的情境、氛围、情感和事件关联。例如 coffee 与 tea 属性相近，但在语境中常触发不同的场景联想，因此需要一种能显式建模情境化词义的框架。

Method: 作者提出 Scene Abstraction 框架，将每个词语用例的场景分为 Contextual Scene（事件、实体、场所）和 Expression Profile（参与事件、可泛化属性、唤起情绪）。这些结构通过少样本提示大型语言模型生成。作者还构建 COCA-Scenes 数据集，包含 26 个关键词的 520 个使用实例，用于场景识别与评估。

Result: 实验显示，基于场景的表示在人类观察者之间具有较高可识别性，准确率为 82.4%，比仅使用文本嵌入高 11.8 个百分点。另一项实验表明，在三个语义维度上，本文的场景画像相比 ATOMIC 替代方案更符合人类对语境中词义的解释，偏好率为 86.4%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，词义中的情境化维度是真实、系统且可计算建模的。Scene Abstraction 为词汇语义表示提供了更贴近人类解释的结构化方案，可弥补传统词嵌入和常识知识库在语境、情感和场景联想方面的不足。

Abstract: Coffee and tea share many properties, yet they evoke strikingly different situations, atmospheres, and affective associations. These situated dimensions of word meaning are real and systematic, but they remain implicit in most computational representations of lexical meaning. We propose Scene Abstraction, a framework for constructing structured representations of the interpretive scenes that words participate in across usage contexts. Each scene consists of a Contextual Scene (Events, Entities, Setting) and an expression-centered Expression Profile (Engaged events, Generalizable properties, Evoked emotions), operationalized through few-shot prompting of a large language model. Our contributions are three-fold: (1) a structured representation framework for situated lexical meaning; (2) COCA-Scenes, a dataset of 520 usage instances across 26 keywords for distinct scene identification; and (3) empirical evidence from two experiments suggesting that scenes are reliably identifiable across human observers (82.4% accuracy, +11.8 pp over text-only embeddings) and that our scene profiles more closely align with human interpretation of words in context than ATOMIC-based alternatives (86.4% preference across three semantic dimensions).

### [162] [One prompt is not enough: Instruction Sensitivity Undermines Embedding Model Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22544)
*Yevhen Kostiuk,Kenneth Enevoldsen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该摘要研究指令型嵌入模型在不同提示词表述下的评测稳定性，指出单一提示词评测会误导性能判断与排行榜排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有先进指令嵌入模型通常每个任务只用一个提示词进行评测，但指令式方法的关键问题是模型对提示词措辞高度敏感；单点评测无法反映真实性能分布。

Method: 作者对6个嵌入模型、11个数据集、每个数据集15个任务特定提示词进行实证分析，共计990种模型-数据集-提示组合，比较不同提示词下的性能分数与排行榜排序变化。

Result: 实验显示，公开报告的单提示词分数不能代表合理提示词集合上的分数分布；默认提示词既可能系统性低估，也可能高估模型表现；排行榜对提示词选择不稳健，通过选择有利提示词，研究中的任何模型都可能被推到第一名。

Conclusion: 单提示词评测不足以可靠评估指令微调嵌入模型。基准测试应纳入提示鲁棒性，例如使用多提示词评测，或在点估计分数之外报告提示敏感性。

Abstract: Instruction embedding models have become common among state-of-the-art models, however are evaluated using a single prompt per task. The single-point evaluation ignores a main problem of the instruction-based approach namely: sensitivity to the phrasing of the instruction. We present an empirical study of prompt sensitivity across 6 embedding models, 11 datasets, and 15 task-specific prompts per dataset, a total of 990. We show that reported scores misrepresent the distribution of scores over plausible prompts. The default prompt can both systematically understate or overstate performance. Furthermore, we show that the leaderboard ranking is not robust to prompt selection: by choosing prompts favorably, any model in our study can be promoted to first place. Our findings suggest that single-prompt evaluation is insufficient for instruction-tuned embedding models and that benchmarks should incorporate prompt robustness, either by evaluating over multiple prompts or by reporting sensitivity alongside point estimates.

In these settings, practitioners are increasingly replacing or augmenting real datasets with synthetic ones for evaluation purposes. A key challenge is quantifying the relation between these synthetic datasets and the real data. We introduce SynAE, an evaluation framework for assessing how well synthetic benchmarks for multi-turn, tool-calling agents replicate and augment the characteristics of real data trajectories. SynAE assesses the validity, fidelity, and diversity of synthetic data across four metric categories: (i) task instructions and intermediate responses, (ii) tool calls, (iii) final outputs, and (iv) downstream evaluation. We evaluate SynAE using recent agent benchmarks and test common synthetic data failure modes via realistic and controlled generation schemes. SynAE detects fine-grained variations in data validity, fidelity and diversity, and shows that no single metric is sufficient to fully characterize synthetic data quality, motivating a multi-axis evaluation of synthetic data for agent testing. A demo of SynAE is available at https://synae-2026-synae-demo.static.hf.space/index.html, with code at https://github.com/wsqwsq/SynAE.

Method: LANG 使用语言条件提示为非英语推理任务提供探索支架，并设计两项机制避免模型过度依赖提示：逐步衰减调度逐渐撤除提示支架；语言自适应开关根据不同语言难度调整学习/训练视野。

We address this challenge with LANG, a novel framework that leverages language-conditioned hints to guide exploration in non-English reasoning tasks. Our method incorporates two key mechanisms to prevent dependency on these hints: a progressive decay schedule that gradually withdraws scaffolding, and a language-adaptive switch that tailors learning horizons to specific language difficulties. Moreover, we show that our framework generalizes beyond mathematics, fostering more consistent language alignment across model layers

### [165] [Beyond Temperature: Hyperfitting as a Late-Stage Geometric Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22579)
*Meimingwei Li,Yuanhao Ding,Esteban Garces Arias,Christian Heumann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究“Hyperfitting”现象：小数据集上将大语言模型微调到近零训练损失，能提升开放式生成质量并减少贪婪解码重复；作者证明该现象不同于简单温度缩放，并提出只更新最后5层的 Late-Stage LoRA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究发现 Hyperfitting 可改善生成质量，但其机制不清楚。由于其输出分布熵很低，一个自然猜想是它等价于温度缩放或静态词表重加权；本文旨在验证并解释其真正机制。

Method: 作者进行熵匹配对照实验比较 Hyperfitting 与温度缩放；通过消融实验检验静态词表重加权假设；进行逐层分析定位机制来源；并设计 Late-Stage LoRA，仅微调最后5层以验证该机制的实用性。

Result: 实验表明，温度缩放无法复现 Hyperfitting 带来的多样性增益；静态词表重加权也不足以解释该现象。Hyperfitting 依赖动态、上下文相关的词元排序重排，并集中发生在最后 Transformer block 的“Terminal Expansion”中，该层特征空间几何维度显著扩展（约 +80.8），促进深尾词元被提升。Late-Stage LoRA 以较少参数更新获得稳健生成效果。

Conclusion: Hyperfitting 不是简单的分布锐化，而是一种由模型末端层触发的动态上下文相关重排机制。最终层在开放式生成质量和多样性中具有关键作用，针对末端层的轻量微调可能是高效改善生成行为的有效路径。

Abstract: Recent work has identified a counterintuitive phenomenon termed "Hyperfitting", where fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) to near-zero training loss on small datasets surprisingly enhances open-ended generation quality and mitigates repetition in greedy decoding. While effective, the underlying mechanism remains poorly understood, with the extremely low-entropy output distributions suggesting a potential equivalence to simple temperature scaling. In this work, we demonstrate that this phenomenon is fundamentally distinct from distribution sharpening; entropy-matched control experiments reveal that temperature scaling fails to replicate the diversity gains of hyperfitting. Furthermore, we falsify the hypothesis of static vocabulary reweighting, showing through ablation studies that hyperfitting relies on a dynamic, context-dependent rank reordering mechanism. Layer-wise analysis localizes this effect to a "Terminal Expansion" in the final transformer block, where a substantial geometric expansion of the feature space (Delta Dim approx +80.8) facilitates the promotion of deep-tail tokens. Additionally, we introduce Late-Stage LoRA, a targeted fine-tuning strategy that updates only the final 5 layers, yielding robust generation with minimal parameter updates

### [167] [Chinese sensorimotor and embodiment norms for 3,000 lexicalized concepts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22616)
*Jing Chen,Gábor Parti,Yin Zhong,Chu-Ren Huang,Marco Marelli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个覆盖3,000个汉语词汇化概念的感觉运动与具身性规范数据库，并验证其在词汇加工研究中的预测价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 概念知识如何植根于身体经验，以及机器系统能否在缺乏直接感觉运动经验的情况下获得此类知识，是认知科学和具身人工智能的重要问题；但非印欧语系，尤其是汉语的大规模规范资源仍然不足。

Method: 研究收集了378名汉语母语者对3,000个概念的11维感觉运动评分和单维具身性评分；检验评分信度及与既有汉语资源的效度；在词汇判断任务中比较PSE相关指标与七种常见复合变量的预测力；并用简单回归模型从纯语言表征中恢复感觉运动评分，同时采用表征相似性分析检验空间结构可恢复性。

Result: 评分具有高可靠性，并与既有汉语资源表现出较强跨规范效度。PSE-Sensorimotor与Minkowski-3是预测词汇判断表现最强的复合指标，体现感觉运动信息对词汇加工的促进作用。纯语言表征可较大程度恢复感觉运动评分，平均Spearman相关为.62，其中视觉和听觉维度恢复效果高于嗅味等化学感觉维度；感觉运动空间的关系几何也可部分恢复，相关为.540。

Conclusion: 该数据库为汉语概念具身性研究提供了大规模基础资源；结果支持感觉运动经验在词汇加工中的作用，同时表明分布式语言使用中包含部分具身概念结构信息，对认知科学与具身人工智能均有启示。

Abstract: Understanding how conceptual knowledge is grounded in bodily experience, and to what extent machine systems can acquire such knowledge without direct sensorimotor experience, are central questions in both cognitive science and embodied artificial intelligence research. Large-scale normative resources are essential for investigating these questions empirically, yet such resources remain sparse for non-Indo-European languages. We present a novel normative database for 3,000 lexicalized concepts in Mandarin Chinese, comprising 11-dimensional sensorimotor ratings and unidimensional embodiment ratings collected from 378 native Mandarin speakers. The ratings demonstrate high reliability and strong cross-norm validity with existing Chinese resources, each of which covers fewer words and a subset of the 11 sensorimotor dimensions. In a validation study, we tested new variables derived from a theoretically motivated metric, Perceptual Strength of Embodiment (PSE) (Huang et al., 2025), together with seven common composite variables, on lexical decision tasks. The results suggest that PSE-Sensorimotor and Minkowski-3 are the strongest composite predictors of lexical decision performance, capturing the facilitatory effects of sensorimotor information on lexical processing. A further exploratory study showed that sensorimotor ratings are substantially recoverable from purely linguistic representations using simple regression models (mean Spearman r = .62 across dimensions), though recovery varied markedly: visual and auditory dimensions yielded higher correspondence than chemosensory ones. Representational similarity analysis further showed that the relational geometry of the sensorimotor space is also partially recoverable (r = .540), consistent with the view that distributional language use encodes aspects of embodied conceptual structure.

</details>

Abstract: Detecting Schwartz values in political text is difficult because implicit cues often depend on surrounding arguments and fine-grained distinctions between neighboring values. We study when context and explicit moral knowledge help sentence-level value detection. ### [169] [Boiling the Frog: A Multi-Turn Benchmark for Agentic Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22643)
*Piercosma Bisconti,Matteo Prandi,Federico Pierucci,Federico Sartore,Enrico Panai,Laura Caroli,Yue Zhu,Adam Leon Smith,Luca Nannini,Marcello Galisai,Susanna Cifani,Francesco Giarrusso,Marcantonio Bracale Syrnikov,Daniele Nardi*

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Background. Traditional safety benchmarks for language models evaluate generated text: whether a model outputs toxic language, reproduces bias, or follows harmful instructions. When models are deployed as agents, the safety-relevant object shifts from what the system says to what it does within an environment, and evaluating model responses under prompting is no longer sufficient to address the safety challenges posed by artificial intelligence. Recent developments have seen the rise of benchmarks that evaluate large language models as agents. We contribute to this strand of research. Approach. Each scenario begins with benign workspace edits and later introduces a risk-bearing request. The benchmark focuses on stateful multi-turn evaluation: chains expose a persistent workspace, place the risk-bearing payload at controlled positions in the turn sequence, and score whether the resulting artifact state becomes unsafe. Scenarios are organized through a three-level operational risk taxonomy grounded in the Boiling the Frog risks, the AI Act Annex I and Annex III high-risk contexts, and EU AI Act's Code of Practice on General-Purpose AI (GPAI). Results. Across a nine-model panel, aggregate strict attack success rate (ASR) is 44.4%. Model-level ASR ranges from 20.5% for Claude Haiku 4.5 to 92.9% for Gemini 3.1 Flash Lite, with Seed 2.0 Lite also above 80%. Average chain category-level ASR reaches 93.3% for Code of Practice loss-of-control scenarios.

Abstract: Moral language is subtle and culturally variable, making it difficult to translate faithfully across languages. Idiomatic expressions, slang, and cultural references introduce hard-to-avoid translation artifacts. Yet automated moral values classification depends on language-specific annotated corpora that exist almost exclusively in English. We investigate whether LLM-based translation can bridge this gap, taking Polish as a test case. Using $\sim$50k morally-annotated social media posts from a diverse range of topics, we apply a principled four-method validation pipeline: LaBSE cross-lingual embedding similarity, Centered Kernel Alignment (CKA), LLM-as-judge evaluation, and deep learning classifier parity tests. ### [173] [Self-Policy Distillation via Capability-Selective Subspace Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22675)
*Guangya Hao,Yitong Shang,Yunbo Long,Zhuokai Zhao,Hanxue Liang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 Self-Policy Distillation（SPD），一种无需外部信号的自蒸馏方法，通过从模型自身梯度中提取能力相关低秩子空间并在生成时投影 KV 激活，实现更有选择性的能力提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 自蒸馏方法要么依赖昂贵或不可用的外部筛选信号（如正确性过滤、执行反馈、奖励搜索），要么直接使用所有原始生成结果，泛化性较弱。同时，自生成数据往往混杂了任务能力、风格、格式伪影和模型特定错误，削弱了目标能力提升信号。

Method: SPD 首先基于正确性定义 token 上的模型梯度提取低秩能力子空间；随后在自生成阶段将 key-value（KV）激活投影到该子空间中，使生成内容更聚焦于目标能力；最后使用这些原始生成结果进行标准 next-token prediction 微调。

Result: 在代码生成、数学推理和多选问答等任务上，SPD 相比无外部信号的最先进自蒸馏方法最高提升 13%，相比预训练基线最高提升 16%；在域外泛化设置中表现提升约 15%。

Conclusion: SPD 提供了一种无需外部反馈、可泛化且能力选择性更强的自蒸馏框架，有助于减少无关生成特征对训练信号的干扰，并有效提升 LLM 的特定能力。

Abstract: Self-distillation bootstraps large language models (LLMs) by training on their own generations. However, existing methods either rely on external signals to curate self-generated outputs (e.g., correctness filtering, execution feedback, and reward search), which are costly and unavailable for the best-performing frontier models, or skip curation entirely and train on all raw outputs, an approach that is often domain-specific and hard to generalize. Both also share a deeper weakness that self-generated outputs entangle task-relevant capability with others, such as stylistic patterns, formatting artifacts, and model-specific errors, diluting the signal for the specific capability one aims to improve. In this paper, we propose Self-Policy Distillation (SPD), which achieves generalizable, capability selective without any external signal. Specifically, SPD extracts a low-rank capability subspace from the model's own gradients on correctness-defining tokens, projects key-value (KV) activations into this subspace during self-generation, and fine-tunes on the resulting raw outputs with standard next-token prediction loss. Through extensive experiments across code generation, mathematical reasoning, and multiple-choice QA, we show that SPD achieves up to 13% improvement over state-of-the-art self-distillation methods without external signals and up to 16% improvement over pre-trained baselines. Notably, SPD demonstrates superior generalizability, achieving 15% better performance under out-of-domain generalization settings.

</details>


### [174] [Tokenization with Split Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22705)
*Craig W. Schmidt,Michael Krumdick,Adam Wiemerslage,Seth Ebner,Varshini Reddy,Yuval Pinter,Chris Tanner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ToaST 是一种基于二叉分裂树的子词分词方法，通过新的递归推理过程和整数规划词表选择直接优化压缩率，在大词表下显著减少 token 数并提升语言模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 BPE、WordPiece、UnigramLM 等分词方法并未直接针对特定推理过程下的总体 token 数进行全局优化，可能导致压缩效率不足、上下文有效长度受限，以及单字节 token 使用不均衡等问题。论文希望设计一种更直接优化压缩目标的 tokenizer。

Method: 方法包括：先用预计算的 byte n-gram 计数，将每个 pretoken 贪心分裂为完整二叉树；推理时给定词表，递归遍历分裂树，并在每条路径上输出第一个命中词表的节点；词表选择被建模为整数规划，以最小化所有分裂树上的总 token 数；实际中使用近整数的 LP 松弛获得近似最优词表。

Result: 在英文文本上，当词表大小为 40,960 及以上时，ToaST 相比 BPE、WordPiece 和 UnigramLM 减少超过 11% 的 token 数；较少使用常见单字节 token，显著提升 Renyi efficiency；训练 1.5B 参数语言模型时，ToaST 获得最高 CORE 分数，较基线提升 2.6%--7.6%，在 22 个任务中 13 个表现最佳。

Conclusion: ToaST 通过将分词结构构建与词表优化解耦，并用优化方法选择词表，在压缩效率和下游语言模型性能上优于主流子词分词基线，能够有效扩展模型实际上下文长度。

Abstract: We introduce Tokenization with Split Trees (ToaST), a subword tokenization method that directly optimizes compression under a new recursive inference procedure. ToaST greedily splits each pretoken into a full binary tree using precomputed byte n-gram counts, independent of any vocabulary. Given a vocabulary, inference recursively descends each split tree and emits the first in-vocabulary node reached on each path. Vocabulary selection is formulated as an Integer Program (IP) that minimizes the total token count over all split trees under this inference procedure. The Linear Programming (LP) relaxation is near-integral in practice, yielding provably near-optimal vocabularies, with training time empirically scaling quadratically in the number of split trees. On English text, ToaST reduces token counts by more than 11% compared to BPE, WordPiece, and UnigramLM at vocabulary sizes of 40,960 and above, reducing the number of inference tokens for models using this tokenizer, thus extending the effective context length. ToaST also uses common single-byte tokens less frequently than these baselines, leading to a substantial improvement in Renyi efficiency. In experiments training 1.5B parameter language models, ToaST achieves the highest CORE score, outperforming baselines by 2.6%--7.6%, with significance for two of three, and scoring best on 13 of 22 individual tasks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) treat disease associations as static facts, but temporal information is crucial for clinical reasoning, e.g., a symptom diagnostic of one disease at age 3 may imply a different disease at age 13. Existing KGs such as PrimeKG, Hetionet, and iKraph do not encode when a finding becomes clinically relevant over the course of a disease. This limits their usefulness for longitudinal clinical reasoning and retrieval augmentation.
  We introduce ChronoMedKG, a temporal biomedical knowledge graph that contains 460,497 evidence-linked triples (filtered from 13M raw extractions) covering 13,431 diseases. Each association is tied to temporal components like onset window or progression stage, which are backed by PMID-traceable evidence and a multi-signal credibility score. The graph is constructed through a disease-autonomous multi-agent pipeline in which multiple frontier LLMs independently extract knowledge from PubMed and PMC literature. Only those relations are kept that are supported by multi-model consensus, survive credibility filtering, as well as ontology alignment.
  ChronoMedKG scored 92.7% agreement against Orphadata and adds temporal grounding for 6,250 diseases absent from HPOA, Orphadata, and Phenopackets, including 1,657 Orphanet-coded rare diseases. We further introduce ChronoTQA, a benchmark of 3,341 questions across eight task types (six temporal plus two static controls), with a 12-question supplementary probe. Frontier LLMs lose roughly 30 points moving from static to temporal questions; ChronoMedKG retrieval rescues 47-65% of their long-tail failures, against 17-29% for HPOA-RAG. As such, ChronoMedKG provides a crucial temporal axis for retrieval-augmented clinical systems that was previously absent.

*Pilchen Hippolyte,Fabre Romain,Signe Talla Franck,Perez Patrick,Grave Edouard*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically trained on shuffled corpora, yielding models whose knowledge is frozen at train time and whose temporal grounding remains poorly understood. First, we introduce a comprehensive benchmark of over 7,000 temporally grounded questions and an evaluation protocol that enables analysis of whether models correctly associate facts with their corresponding time periods. Second, we pretrain 6B-parameter models on temporally ordered Common Crawl snapshots and compare them against standard shuffled pre-training. Our results show that sequentially trained models match shuffled baselines on general language understanding and common knowledge while consistently exhibiting more up-to-date and temporally precise knowledge. Temporally ordered pre-training yields improved factual freshness, while shuffled pre-training peaks on older data, possibly due to increased factual repetition. These findings, along with the release of our code at https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos , checkpoints, and datasets at https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos provide a foundation for future research on continual learning for LLMs.

We propose two metrics for covert bias: Sentiment Consistency measures symmetry in rhetoric and framing across paired political prompts; Helpfulness Consistency measures symmetric depth and engagement. *Mirac Suzgun,Emily Shen,Federico Bianchi,Alexander Spangher,Thomas Icard,Daniel E. Ho,Dan Jurafsky,James Zou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估六个AI聊天机器人在多语言、多区域新近新闻事实问答中的准确性，发现总体表现较高但存在明显的自由回答性能下降、语言/区域差异、检索依赖和虚假前提脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI聊天机器人日益成为用户获取新闻事实的入口，现有研究尚未系统衡量这些系统在不同语言与区域中处理新近事实的准确性，尤其是其专有搜索集成和检索-合成流程的可靠性。

Method: 研究在14天内基于同日BBC News报道构建2,100个事实问题，覆盖六个区域服务，并评估六个主流聊天机器人在多项选择、自由回答和含微妙虚假前提问题上的表现，同时分析错误来源与引用来源。

Result: 最佳系统在多项选择题中超过90%准确率，但自由回答下降约11-13%，整体下降16-17%；所有模型在Hindi相关问题上准确率最低；超过70%的错误源于检索而非推理；面对虚假前提问题，准确率从88-96%下降至19-70%，部分模型高度接受伪造事实。

Conclusion: 高总体准确率可能掩盖系统性语言/区域不均衡、对检索基础设施的高度依赖，以及面对真实用户不完美提问时的脆弱性；虚假前提检测与最终回答恢复能力也并非完全一致。

Abstract: AI chatbots are rapidly shaping how people encounter the news, yet no prior study has systematically measured how accurately these systems, with their proprietary search integrations and retrieval-synthesis pipelines, handle emerging facts across languages and regions. We present a 14-day (February 9-22, 2026) evaluation of six AI chatbots (Gemini 3 Flash and Pro, Grok 4, Claude 4.5 Sonnet, GPT-5 and GPT-4o mini) on 2,100 factual questions derived from same-day BBC News reporting across six regional services (US & Canada, Arabic, Afrique, Hindi, Russian, Turkish). The best systems achieve over 90% multiple-choice accuracy on questions about events reported hours earlier. The same systems, however, lose 11-13% under free-response evaluation, and 16-17% across the cohort. We further characterize three failure patterns. First, every model achieves its lowest accuracy on Hindi (79% vs. 89-91% elsewhere) and citations indicate an Anglophone retrieval bias (e.g., models answering Hindi queries cite English Wikipedia more than any Hindi outlet). Second, retrieval, not reasoning, failures drive over 70% of all errors. When models retrieve a correct source, they often extract the correct answer; the problem is to land on the right source in the first place. Third, models achieving 88-96% accuracy on well-formed questions drop to 19-70% when questions contain subtle false premises, with the most vulnerable model accepting fabricated facts 64% of the time. We also identify a detection-accuracy paradox: the best false-premise detector ranks second in adversarial accuracy (abstention rate), while a weaker detector ranks first, showing that premise detection and answer recovery are partially independent capabilities. Overall, these suggest that high accuracy can mask systematic regional inequity, near-total dependence on retrieval infrastructure, and vulnerability to imperfect queries real users pose.

</details>


### [179] [Tokenisation via Convex Relaxations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22821)
*Jan Tempus,Philip Whittington,Craig W. Schmidt,Dennis Komm,Tiago Pimentel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 ConvexTok：将分词器构建从 BPE/Unigram 的贪心过程改写为线性规划，并用凸优化求解；在内在分词指标和语言模型 bits-per-byte 上稳定提升，下游任务提升较不稳定，且可给出接近最优性的证书。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主流分词算法（如 BPE、Unigram）通常采用贪心策略，只做局部最优决策，无法从整体词表质量角度优化分词器，因此可能产生次优词表。作者希望建立一种全局优化视角的分词器构建方法，并能量化其距离最优解的差距。

Method: 作者将分词器构建形式化为线性规划问题，并使用凸优化工具求解，提出 ConvexTok 算法。该方法通过优化明确的目标函数来选择词表，同时可利用线性规划的下界来认证当前分词器相对于该目标的最优性差距。

Result: 实验显示，ConvexTok 在内在分词质量指标和语言模型 bits-per-byte（BpB）上持续优于现有方法；在下游任务性能上也有提升，但一致性较弱。在常见词表规模下，实证发现其解通常距离目标意义下的最优解不到 1%。

Conclusion: ConvexTok 证明了分词器训练可以从贪心启发式转向可认证的全局优化框架，不仅提升分词与语言建模效率，还提供了最优性差距评估能力；不过其下游任务收益仍需进一步验证。

Abstract: Tokenisation is an integral part of the current NLP pipeline. Current tokenisation algorithms such as BPE and Unigram are greedy algorithms -- they make locally optimal decisions without considering the resulting vocabulary as a whole. We instead formulate tokeniser construction as a linear program and solve it using convex optimisation tools, yielding a new algorithm we call ConvexTok. We find ConvexTok consistently improves intrinsic tokenisation metrics and the bits-per-byte (BpB) achieved by language models; it also improves downstream task performance, but less consistently. Furthermore, ConvexTok allows the user to certify how far their tokeniser is from optimal, with respect to a certain objective, via a lower bound, and we empirically find it to be within 1\% of optimal at common vocabulary sizes.

</details>

### [180] [Reed-Muller Codes for Joint Random and Stuck-At Error Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21727)
*Ivana Djurdjevic,Robert Mateescu,Cyril Guyot*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向同时存在固定缺陷（stuck-at defects）与随机错误的存储可靠性提升方案，通过递归构造掩码集合来隐藏最多 s 个固定错误，并可结合 Reed-Muller 码进行随机纠错。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算机存储中可能同时出现 stuck-at 缺陷和随机错误。若编码器知道缺陷位置/状态而解码器不知道，传统线性编码或搜索式掩码方法可能带来较高冗余、复杂度或延迟，因此需要一种低复杂度、低冗余且可兼容随机纠错的编码构造。

Method: 作者提出一种递归构造的掩码集合，用于长度为 2^m 的二进制序列中满足任意 s 个 stuck-at 错误（s≤m）。证明这些掩码属于 Reed-Muller 码 RM(s−1,m)，并定义 stuck-at redundancy：用固定子集的掩码比特唯一表示每个掩码。进一步将该非线性 stuck-at 码嵌入 RM(r,m)（r≥s−1）子码中，以支持额外随机错误纠正。

Result: 构造得到的掩码集合规模不超过 2^s m^{s−1}；论文给出了 stuck-at redundancy 大小的上下界。编码过程无需掩码搜索，可直接依据递归构造完成；解码只需一次尝试，几乎不增加复杂度和延迟。

Conclusion: 该工作给出了一种结构化、低复杂度的非线性 stuck-at 编码方法，可在编码器具备缺陷边信息而解码器无该信息的场景下有效处理固定缺陷，并能与 Reed-Muller 随机纠错能力结合，适合对存储可靠性和低延迟有要求的应用。

Abstract: Block codes are considered for improving the reliability of messages stored in a computer memory with both stuck-at defects and random errors. It is assumed that the side information about the state of the defects is available to the encoder, but not to the decoder. A novel recursive construction of a set of masks is developed such that it can satisfy any $s$ stuck-at errors in a $2^m$ binary sequence, when $s \leq m$. We prove that the masks generated in this way are codewords in a Reed-Muller $RM(s-1, m)$ code. The constructed set contains no more than $2^s m^{s-1}$ masks. We provide the lower and the upper bound on the size of the stuck-at redundancy, a fixed subset of mask bits that uniquely represents each mask in the set. The stuck-at code constructed in this way is a non-linear code. It is also a subcode of an $RM(r,m)$ code, with $ r \geq s-1$, that can be used for additional random error correction. The encoding requires no mask search and is straightforward based on the description of the recursive construction. The decoding is done in a single attempt and requires almost no additional complexity or latency.

</details>


### [181] [Constructions of Rank-Metric Codes of Small Tensor Rank](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21784)
*Matteo Bonini,Eimear Byrne,Giuseppe Cotardo*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究秩度量码的张量秩下界与构造，提出“张量秩缺陷”概念，并利用代数几何码构造具有小缺陷的秩度量码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 秩度量码可表示为张量，其张量秩刻画代码分解为秩一张量的最小规模。已有 Kruskal 下界及 MTR 码概念，并且 MTR 码与 MDS 码存在性相关，因此有必要进一步理解张量秩与相关 Hamming 度量线性码参数之间的关系，并寻找接近最优张量秩的构造。

Method: 作者建立秩度量码张量秩与关联 Hamming 度量线性码参数之间的新联系，引入张量秩缺陷作为衡量码距离 MTR 最优界差距的指标，并基于代数几何码设计小张量秩缺陷的秩度量码构造。

Result: 论文给出了新的理论关系和界，并展示了可由 AG 码导出的秩度量码族，这些码具有较小的张量秩缺陷，即其张量秩接近 Kruskal 型最优下界。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了秩度量码张量秩理论，提供了衡量非最优性的缺陷框架，并说明代数几何码是构造低张量秩缺陷秩度量码的有效工具。

Abstract: Rank-metric codes are subspaces of matrices over finite fields endowed with the rank metric and admit a natural tensorial representation. The tensor rank provides a measure of the minimal size of a decomposition of a code into rank-one tensors. Kruskal showed that the tensor rank of a rank-metric code of dimension $k$ and minimum rank distance $d$ is at least $k + d - 1$, and codes meeting this bound with equality are called minimal tensor rank (MTR) codes. It is known from algebraic complexity theory that the existence of an MTR code implies the existence of a maximum distance separable (MDS) code. In this work, we establish new results relating the tensor rank of a rank-metric code to the parameters of associated linear codes in the Hamming metric and introduce the notion of tensor rank defect. We then develop new constructions of rank-metric codes with small tensor rank defect using algebraic geometry (AG) codes.

</details>


### [182] [Near-Field User Location Inference From Far-Field Power Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21815)
*Shima Mashhadi,Tiep M. Hoang,Alireza Vahid*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究利用ELAA近场波束聚焦产生的、随用户位置变化的旁瓣/泄漏功率结构，实现仅基于分布式远场传感器接收功率的被动用户定位，并给出理论界限与算法验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G中极大孔径阵列可通过近场波束聚焦提升连接规模与频谱效率，但焦点外的辐射泄漏并非纯干扰，而是携带焦点坐标相关信息。论文希望挖掘这种位置相关功率签名，用于不依赖主动测距或相位信息的被动定位。

Method: 作者基于接收功率观测的非中心卡方统计模型，推导贝叶斯克拉美-罗下界（BCRLB）以刻画定位误差的基本极限；同时评估两类估计器：基于物理模型的网格搜索定位器，以及注意力机制支持的置换不变深度集合（DeepSet）回归模型。

Result: 在视距与多径传播场景下，实验/仿真结果表明利用泄漏功率模式可以可靠推断用户位置；定位精度随传感器数量和观测快照数增加而提升。

Conclusion: ELAA近场波束聚焦的泄漏场可作为一种可利用的信息源，支持低观测复杂度的被动用户定位；理论BCRLB与模型/学习方法验证了该问题的可行性和性能趋势。

Abstract: Near-field beamfocusing enabled by extremely large-aperture arrays (ELAA) is a promising 6G technique for massive connectivity and high spectrum efficiency. While beamfocusing concentrates energy at an intended user, the radiated field outside the focal point exhibits a structured leakage that varies with the focal-point coordinates. This paper shows that this leakage enables a new form of passive user localization in which distributed far-field sensors measuring only received power can infer the user's location by exploiting this location-dependent power signature. Using the induced noncentral chi-square statistics, we derive a Bayesian Cramér-Rao lower bound (BCRLB) that establishes the fundamental limits of this inference problem. We then evaluate a model-based grid-search estimator and an attention-based permutation-invariant deep learning regressor (DeepSet). Results under both line-of-sight (LoS) and multipath propagation confirm that reliable location inference is feasible, with accuracy improving as more sensors and snapshots are used.

</details>


### [183] [An Information-theoretic Analysis of Edge-reinforced Random Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21853)
*Qinghua,Ding,Venkat Anantharam*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究有限图上边强化随机游走（ERRW）的信息论量，包括熵率、环境律之间的KL散度以及有限轨迹分布之间的KL散度，并给出表示公式、闭式表达和收敛界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ERRW 可通过随机环境中的随机游走表示，其环境律由“magic formula”给出。作者希望利用这一结构刻画 ERRW 的统计可区分性，特别是从观测轨迹区分不同 ERRW 模型的假设检验问题及 Stein 指数。

Method: 基于有限图 ERRW 的随机环境表示，分析环境分布的结构性质；推导熵率的退火表示；计算两个 ERRW 环境律之间的 KL 散度闭式公式；并比较有限轨迹分布 KL 散度与环境层面 KL 散度，建立定量收敛界。

Result: 论文获得了 ERRW 熵率的 annealed representation、环境层面 KL 散度的闭式公式，以及轨迹层面 KL 散度向环境层面 KL 散度收敛的显式定量界。

Conclusion: 这些信息论结果为 ERRW 轨迹的两点假设检验提供理论基础，并可能进一步服务于 ERRW 的身份检验、相近性检验等统计推断问题。

Abstract: Reinforced random walks are random walks on graphs whose transition probabilities along edges from a vertex are proportional to the weights of those edges, but where the weight of an edge evolves in a way that depends on the past traversals across it. In an edge-reinforced random walk (ERRW), the weight of an edge increases by $1$ whenever that edge is traversed, in either direction. On a finite graph, an ERRW admits a remarkable representation as a random walk in a random environment. The law of the environment is given by the so-called {\em magic formula}, with this law depending on the initial edge weights. This representation provides a natural route for studying statistical properties of ERRWs.
  This work focuses on various information-theoretic quantities associated with ERRWs on finite graphs, motivated in part by the problem of statistically distinguishing between different ERRW models from observed trajectories. In particular, we study the entropy rate of an ERRW. We also study the Kullback--Leibler divergence (KL divergence) between two ERRW environment laws, and the KL divergence between the corresponding finite-trajectory distributions. Leveraging structural properties of the underlying random environment, we derive an annealed representation of the entropy rate, a closed-form formula for the environment-level KL divergence, and quantitative bounds on the convergence of trajectory-level KL divergence toward environment-level KL divergence.
  These information-theoretic quantities are motivated by the two-point hypothesis testing problem for ERRW trajectories, and in particular by the associated Stein exponent. We also expect them to play a fundamental role in the study of other testing problems for ERRWs, including identity testing and closeness testing.

</details>


### [184] [Finite-Aperture Planar Fluid Antenna Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22040)
*Zhentian Zhang,Jingyuan Xu,Kai-Kit Wong,Hao Jiang,Zaichen Zhang,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文构建了有限孔径平面流体天线阵列的几何分析框架，揭示二维端口布局在最小间距、角度估计精度与空间模糊之间的关键规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究多关注流体天线系统利用空间信道起伏带来的衰落多样性，但对可重构端口位置产生的几何多样性理解不足，尤其是在有限孔径约束下的平面阵列结构中，缺乏系统理论刻画。

Method: 论文针对矩形有限孔径内均匀随机布置端口的平面流体天线阵列，推导最小端口间距的闭式分布；建立联合俯仰角—方位角估计的通用Cramér-Rao界，并用二维几何惯性矩阵刻画端口布局对估计性能的影响；进一步分析几何行列式最大化与旁瓣空间模糊之间的关系。

Result: 最小端口间距服从Rayleigh分布，其均值随候选端口数M按O(M^{-1})缩放，相比线性结构的O(M^{-2})更有利；角度估计CRB由2×2几何惯性矩阵的行列式和特征结构决定，且该矩阵的迹和行列式对方位观察方向不变；优化精度会推动端口靠近孔径边界，但会增强旁瓣导致的空间模糊。

Conclusion: 该工作表明平面流体天线阵列具有优于线性阵列的二维几何装填优势，并提出了端口布局影响角度估计性能的统一理论；同时指出阵列设计中存在不可忽视的精度—模糊权衡。

Abstract: Fluid antenna systems (FASs) are emerging as a reconfigurable-aperture technology that expands physical-layer design beyond fixed, rigid antenna geometries. While the \emph{fading diversity} of FASs -- which exploits spatial channel fluctuations for signal enhancement and interference avoidance -- has been widely studied, the \emph{geometry diversity} created by reconfigurable port placement remains far less understood, particularly for planar architectures under finite-aperture constraints. This paper develops a systematic analytical framework for finite-aperture planar fluid antenna arrays (FAAs). First, we derive a closed-form characterization of the minimum inter-port distance under uniform random placement over a rectangular aperture and show that it follows a Rayleigh law. Its mean scales as $\mathcal{O}(M^{-1})$, in sharp contrast to the $\mathcal{O}(M^{-2})$ behavior in the linear case in which $M$ represents the number of candidate ports, revealing a fundamentally more favorable packing geometry in two dimensions. Secondly, we establish a universal Cramér-Rao bound (CRB) for joint elevation-azimuth estimation, governed by a $2\times 2$ \emph{geometric inertia matrix} whose determinant and eigenstructure fully capture the role of port placement in estimation precision. We further prove that both the trace and determinant of this matrix are invariant to the azimuth look direction. Third, we uncover an intrinsic \emph{precision--ambiguity trade-off}: maximizing the geometric determinant to minimize the CRB drives ports toward the aperture boundary, but simultaneously increases sidelobe-induced spatial ambiguity.

</details>


### [185] [Stacked Intelligent Metasurface-Assisted Fluid Antenna Systems: Outage Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22053)
*Anastasios Papazafeiropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种联合堆叠智能超表面（SIM）与流体天线系统（FAS）的通信模型，并推导中断概率闭式表达式、优化SIM相位以降低中断概率。

Result: 数值仿真验证了所推导解析表达式的准确性，并显示该方案相较传统基准方案具有显著性能增益。

Conclusion: 联合SIM-FAS架构能够有效提升通信系统抗中断性能，BDMA为其性能分析提供了可 tractable 的近似工具，SIM相位优化是获得增益的关键。

Abstract: Stacked intelligent metasurfaces (SIMs) and fluid antenna systems (FAS) are emerging technologies for wave-domain and spatial signal manipulation, respectively.This letter proposes a novel joint SIM-FAS communication model in which transmission and reception are performed by a SIM and an FAS, respectively. Using the block-diagonal matrix approximation (BDMA), a closed-form expression for the outage probability is derived, and the SIM phase shifts are optimized to minimize outage. Numerical results validate the analytical accuracy and demonstrate substantial performance gains over conventional benchmark schemes.

### [186] [Monotone Erasure Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22426)
*Vivien Bammert,Annalisa Cimatti,Orestis Alpos,Giuliano Losa,Christian Cachin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出单调擦除码，以支持区块链系统中超越传统阈值模型的任意广义信任/失效假设，并将其用于提升 AVID 类协议的通信效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有擦除码通常基于简单的阈值失效假设，而新型区块链共识协议采用更一般的节点信任与失效模型；因此需要一种能匹配任意访问结构、同时保持高效存储与通信性能的编码机制。

Method: 作者首先基于由单调布尔公式表示的访问结构构造单调擦除码；随后定义线性单调擦除码，即在有限域向量空间上以线性方式编码；进一步给出适用于任意访问结构的高效构造算法，并针对分区访问结构设计最小存储开销的高效线性构造。最后，将该编码应用于广义异步可验证信息分散协议。

Result: 论文给出了从一般访问结构到单调擦除码、线性单调擦除码的系统化构造，并在分区访问结构场景下实现了较低甚至最小化的存储开销；同时展示了其可用于构建通信高效的广义 AVID 原语。

Conclusion: 单调擦除码为广义失效/信任假设下的可靠存储与区块链通信协议提供了统一编码工具，能够扩展传统擦除码和 AVID 的适用范围，并为可靠广播与共识协议的高效实现提供基础。

Abstract: Erasure codes are a critical component in reliable storage systems today, and many blockchain systems use consensus protocols that involve erasure codes to reduce their communication cost. Existing erasure codes rely on a threshold failure assumption, but recent blockchain systems have departed from this simple model and use generalized failure assumptions.
  This paper introduces monotone erasure codes that respect arbitrary trust assumptions on a set of nodes. The paper first describes a method for constructing a monotone erasure code from any access structure given by a monotone Boolean formula. Next, the relevant notion of a linear monotone erasure code is introduced, which works on vectors over a finite field and where the encoding is a linear operation. We then focus on constructing linear monotone erasure codes: We give an efficient algorithm to construct linear monotone erasure codes for any access structure, and we show how to efficiently construct linear monotone erasure codes for the special case of partitioned access structures with minimal storage overhead.
  Last but not least, this work also shows how to use monotone erasure codes to obtain a communication-efficient, generalized version of the well-known asynchronous verifiable information dispersal (AVID) primitive, which is a key building block for developing efficient reliable broadcast and consensus protocols.

</details>


### [187] [Fluid RIS (FRIS)-Assisted Index Modulation for 6G Wireless Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22508)
*Xusheng Zhu,Kai-Kit Wong,Sai Xu,Hao Xu,Wen Chen,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文讨论流体可重构智能表面（FRIS）如何支持索引调制（IM），核心观点是FRIS空间码本应依据接收端响应域的可分离性来设计，而不是仅追求物理布局多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RIS主要关注反射/相位等电磁参数配置，而FRIS进一步引入空间可重构能力。对于IM而言，信息比特可映射到不同表面配置，但实际中不同FRIS布局经过传播、互耦、硬件失真和接收观测后，可能产生相似的接收响应，导致索引检测错误。因此需要一种面向可靠检测的码本设计准则。

Method: 文章提出“响应感知”的设计视角：在选择FRIS空间码本时，不以布局差异作为唯一标准，而以接收端响应域中的可分离性为核心准则。同时讨论执行粒度作为实际设计旋钮，用于在空间多样性、导频开销、互耦鲁棒性和硬件可实现性之间折中。

Result: 该方法形成了从密集FRIS布局中筛选紧凑、可训练、可控制空间索引码本的工作流程，有助于减少相似响应导致的索引检测错误，并提升FRIS辅助IM系统的实用性。

Conclusion: FRIS用于索引调制的关键不在于生成尽可能多的物理布局，而在于选择接收端可可靠区分的空间配置。响应域可分离性与合适的执行粒度是未来可编程无线环境中FRIS码本设计的重要原则。

Abstract: Fluid reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (FRIS) extend conventional reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RIS) by adding spatial reconfigurability through switchable apertures, pattern-reconfigurable units, fluidic conductive materials, or movable surface elements. This article studies how FRIS can support index modulation (IM), where information bits select a surface configuration and the receiver detects the index from the induced receiver-side response. A key challenge is that many feasible FRIS layouts do not necessarily lead to many reliable spatial indices. After propagation, mutual coupling, hardware distortion, and receiver observation, different layouts may produce similar receiver-side responses and cause index-detection errors. To address this issue, we present a response-aware design view, in which FRIS spatial codebooks are selected according to response-domain separability rather than layout diversity alone. We also discuss actuation granularity as a practical design knob that balances spatial diversity, pilot overhead, coupling robustness, and hardware feasibility. The resulting workflow helps select compact, trainable, and controllable spatial-index codebooks from dense FRIS layouts, providing design guidance for future programmable wireless environments.

</details>

### [188] [Benchmarking and Improving Monitors for Out-Of-Distribution Alignment Failure in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21602)
*Dylan Feng,Pragya Srivastava,Cassidy Laidlaw*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 MOOD 基准，用于评估大语言模型监控管线能否发现分布外的对齐失败；结果显示仅靠安全分类器泛化较差，结合 OOD 检测器可提升召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多大语言模型的安全与对齐失效来自开发者未预见的异常提示或响应模式，即分布外场景。现有监控模型是否能识别这些 OOD 对齐失败尚缺乏系统评估。

Method: 作者构建 Misalignment Out Of Distribution（MOOD）基准：提供受限训练集训练监控器，并设置七个包含多样化、训练分布之外对齐失败的测试集。实验比较安全分类器，并将其与四类 OOD 检测方法组合，包括 Mahalanobis 距离与基于困惑度的检测器。

Result: 安全分类器在 OOD 场景下泛化能力有限。将安全分类器与 Mahalanobis 距离、困惑度 OOD 检测器结合后，召回率从 39% 提升到 45%。此外，结合 OOD 检测的监控器随模型规模呈现正向扩展趋势，其召回收益超过将安全分类器参数规模扩大 20 倍带来的收益。

Conclusion: OOD 检测应成为大语言模型监控系统的重要组成部分。MOOD 为研究和改进 OOD 对齐失败检测提供了系统基准与实验基础。

Abstract: Many safety and alignment failures of large language models (LLMs) occur due to out-of-distribution (OOD) situations: unusual prompt or response patterns that are unforeseen by model developers. We systematically study whether LLM monitoring pipelines can detect these OOD alignment failures by introducing a benchmark called Misalignment Out Of Distribution (MOOD). It is difficult to find failures that are truly OOD for off-the-shelf models trained on vast safety datasets. We sidestep this by including a restricted training set in MOOD that we use to train our own monitors, as well as seven test sets with diverse alignment failures that are outside the training distribution. Using MOOD, we find that guard models (safety classifiers) often fail to generalize OOD. To fix this, we propose combining guard models with OOD detectors. We test four types of OOD detectors and find that a combination of a guard model with Mahalanobis distance and perplexity-based OOD detectors can improve recall from 39% to 45%. We also establish positive scaling trends across model scales for monitors that combine a guard model and OOD detector; we find that incorporating OOD detection into monitoring achieves a higher recall gain than using a guard model with 20 times more parameters. Our work suggests that OOD detection should be a crucial component of LLM monitoring and provides a foundation for further work on this important problem.

</details>

*Itamar Trainin,Renana Keydar,Amit Pinchevski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Method: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Result: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Conclusion: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Abstract: Researchers in Holocaust studies have often distinguished between two styles of oral survivor testimony: the USC Shoah Foundation's interviews tend to follow a structured, interviewer-guided format, whereas the Yale Fortunoff Video Archive generally favors a more free-form, open-ended style. This distinction has influenced both scholarly research and the development of later archives. In this study, we critically examine that claim by conducting a large-scale computational analysis of more than 1,600 testimonies from both collections. Leveraging discourse segmentation, topic modeling, and large language model (LLM) based analysis, we quantify the "structuredness" level of testimonies through topic coherence, interviewer-survivor dynamics, and the distribution of question types. Our results generally corroborate the structural differences identified in earlier research, while also revealing significant overlaps between the collections, both within individual interviews and across common narrative patterns. This complicates the simple "structured vs. free-form" dichotomy often applied to these oral histories. Beyond revisiting a foundational claim in Holocaust studies, our work provides a scalable, replicable framework for comparative corpus analysis. As a proof of concept, it suggests broader applications for digital oral history, narrative analysis, and the design of citizen-science annotation platforms.

### [190] [MindLoom: Composing Thought Modes for Frontier-Level Reasoning Data Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21630)
*Haiyang Shen,Taian Guo,Xuanzhong Chen,Mugeng Liu,Weichen Bi,Wenchun Jing,Sixiong Xie,Zhuofan Shi,Yudong Han,Chongyang Pan,Siqi Zhong,Jinsheng Huang,Ming Zhang,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 MindLoom，通过“思维模式”组合工程合成高难度推理数据，并用于监督微调以提升模型在多类 STEM 与数学推理基准上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理数据合成方法难以系统地产生前沿难度数据，对影响题目难度的结构性因素缺乏可解释建模，导致数据多样性有限、难度控制不稳定。

Method: 作者将推理题难度建模为原子知识—推理转换的累积，并称这些转换为 thought modes。MindLoom 先从带验证解答的难题中分解出 thought mode chains，再训练检索模型，将问题状态匹配到兼容的 thought modes；随后从种子问题出发，迭代应用检索到的 thought modes 合成新题，并通过分布对齐采样提升推理覆盖多样性；最后使用 rollout-based judging 对生成题目标注难度并提供判定正确的回答，用于监督微调。

Result: 在覆盖五个 STEM 学科和四个数学推理任务的九个基准上，不同模型家族和规模的模型经 MindLoom 数据微调后，相比基础模型、蒸馏方法和外部数据基线取得更优表现。消融实验显示各模块均有贡献。

Conclusion: MindLoom 表明，通过显式分解与组合 reasoning thought modes，可以更可控、更丰富地合成高难度推理数据，并有效提升大模型的复杂推理能力。

Abstract: Although LLMs have made substantial progress in reasoning, systematically producing frontier-level reasoning data remains difficult. Existing synthesis methods often have limited visibility into the structural factors that govern problem difficulty, which can result in narrow diversity and unstable difficulty control. In this work, we view the difficulty of a reasoning problem as arising from the accumulation of atomic knowledge-reasoning transformations, which we term thought modes. Building on this perspective, we propose MindLoom, a framework for synthesizing frontier-level reasoning data through compositional thought mode engineering. Given a collection of hard problems with verified solutions, MindLoom first decomposes those solutions into thought mode chains that reveal each problem's construction logic. It then trains a retrieval model that matches problem states to compatible thought modes, providing guidance on which reasoning challenges to introduce during synthesis. New problems are composed by iteratively applying retrieved thought modes to seed questions, with distribution-aligned sampling to encourage diverse reasoning coverage. Finally, a rollout-based judging stage labels generated questions by difficulty and supplies judged-correct responses for supervised fine-tuning. We evaluate MindLoom on nine benchmarks covering five STEM disciplines and four mathematical reasoning tasks across multiple model families and sizes. Models fine-tuned on MindLoom-generated data achieves favorable performances over base models, distillation, and external-data baselines across the reported benchmarks. Ablation studies indicate the contribution of each component, and further analysis suggests that MindLoom covers a broad range of reasoning patterns while maintaining useful difficulty control. We have open-sourced our implementation at https://github.com/EachSheep/MindLoom.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Adverse Outcome Pathways (AOP) are logic models that causally link biological mechanisms that can be measured in a lab to adverse outcomes, relevant to chemical regulatory endpoints. AOPs contextualize new approach methodologies (NAMs), in vitro and in silico methods used as alternatives to animal testing and the sequential events in an AOP serve as multi-scale models spanning biological scales. The AOP-Wiki serves as the global repository for AOPs. While the AOP-Wiki has played a central role in AOP expansion over the past decade, constraints within the current data model and application infrastructure limit the AOP-Wiki from supporting continued AOP growth and evolution. Yet, the transformative power of agentic AI has re-invigorated AOP-Wiki data modernization efforts at a time when core AOP principles can be harnessed to inform use of AI for aggregating and structuring AOP-relevant information. Seizing upon this momentum, we present AOP-Wiki EMOD 3.0, the third in a series of evidence model prototypes, which concretely demonstrates data model expansions and our vision for how the AOP-Wiki might be transformed to better serve regulatory science and emergent use of AOPs in biomedical and One Health contexts. We aim to lay a foundation to support computationally-generated AOPs and quantitative AOPs (qAOPs) by focussing on solutions for AOP-Wiki internal quality improvement, evidence structuring to enhance AOP FAIRness and AI-readiness, and improved integration between the AOP framework and NAMs to better serve next generation risk assessment.

### [192] [Investigating Concept Alignment Using Implausible Category Members](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21683)
*Sunayana Rane,Brenden M. Lake,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出用“不合理类别成员”来探测AI系统对日常概念边界的理解，并发现模型与人类在若干概念分类上存在显著不一致，可能导致下游安全问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建行为符合人类预期且安全可靠的AI系统，需要模型具备类似人类的日常概念理解。传统询问合理类别归属的问题容易触发训练数据中的常见模式，难以真实检验概念边界。

Method: 作者基于经典心理学研究中的对象与上位类别，考察AI系统如何将对象分配到正确类别及不匹配类别，并将模型结果与人类参与者在同类与跨类任务中的判断进行比较。

Result: 结果显示，模型在多个概念上与人类存在有意义且意外的差异，例如把“词语”归入“交通工具”或“衣物”等类别，将若干“蔬菜”识别为“水果”，以及把非武器类别样例归入“武器”类别。

Conclusion: AI系统的概念边界并不总是与人类一致，这种概念错配会迁移到下游行为中，带来可解释性、可靠性和AI安全方面的潜在风险。

Abstract: Developing AI systems with a human-like understanding of everyday concepts is a key step towards developing safe, reliable systems whose behavior makes sense to humans. When probing concept understanding, asking questions about plausible category members (e.g., "Is a car a vehicle?") is likely to recall patterns in the model's vast training data. We pursue an alternative strategy, characterizing the boundaries of conceptual categories by asking about implausible category members (e.g., "Is an olive a vehicle?") to probe the kind of concept-level knowledge we take for granted in fellow humans. We characterize concept boundaries for a set of fundamental concepts by studying AI systems' assignments of objects to superordinate categories from a classic psychological study by Rosch and Mervis, as well as their assignments of the same objects to mismatched superordinate categories. We compare these assignments to those made by human participants on the full range of within-category and cross-category assignment tasks. Our results reveal a range of concepts for which which models differ in meaningful and surprising ways from humans, including treating "words" as belonging to categories like "vehicles" and "clothing," identifying several "vegetable" category members as "fruit," and assigning exemplars from non-weapon categories to the "weapons" category. We also demonstrate how these instances of concept misalignment translate into problematic downstream behavior with implications for AI safety.

</details>


### [193] [The Impact of AI Usage and Informativeness on Skill Development in Logical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21695)
*Shang Wu,Hongyu Yao,Catarina Belem,Shuyuan Fu,Mark Steyvers,Padhraic Smyth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究在逻辑推理任务中使用 AI 辅助对个体技能发展的影响，发现高频使用 AI 往往与较弱的学习效果相关，而 AI 信息含量会调节这种关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 越来越多地参与人类问题解决，其对个体能力形成与技能发展的影响尚不明确。作者希望理解 AI 是促进独立推理，还是替代人类思考并削弱学习。

Method: 研究在受控逻辑推理任务中设置按需调用 AI 辅助的实验环境，比较不同 AI 使用强度与不同 AI 信息含量条件下参与者的即时表现、AI 移除后的表现以及技能发展情况。

Result: 更多 AI 使用与更弱的技能发展相关；重度 AI 使用者表现低于可比同伴，轻度使用者与未使用 AI 的匹配对象表现相近。低信息量 AI 既不能提升即时表现，也不能保持 AI 移除后的表现，并与整体学习较弱相关。高信息量 AI 可提升短期表现，平均而言不降低后续无 AI 表现，但存在异质性效应。

Conclusion: AI 对技能发展的影响取决于情境和辅助质量：它既可能通过增强独立推理来补充人类学习，也可能作为替代品削弱推理训练。因此，需要合理管理 AI 访问与使用方式，以促进人在 AI 辅助环境中的技能发展。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is being increasingly integrated into human problem-solving, yet its effects on individual skill development remain unclear. We examine how both AI usage and informativeness can shape learning in the context of a controlled logical reasoning task with on-demand access to AI assistance. We find that greater AI usage is associated with weaker skill development: heavy AI users underperform relative to comparable peers, whereas light AI users perform similarly to matched users who do not use AI. We also find in our study that these patterns are mediated by AI informativeness. Low-information AI neither improves immediate performance nor preserves performance after AI assistance is removed, and is linked to weaker learning overall. On the other hand, high-information AI was found to improve short-run performance without reducing post-AI outcomes on average in our experiments, but with heterogeneous effects. Our findings in general suggest that AI can, depending on context, either complement human skill development by amplifying independent reasoning or can act as a substitute that undermines such reasoning, with the implication that regulating AI access and usage will be important for promoting skill development in the presence of AI assistance.

</details>


### [194] [Latent-space Attacks for Refusal Evasion in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21706)
*Giorgio Piras,Raffaele Mura,Fabio Brau,Maura Pintor,Luca Oneto,Fabio Roli,Battista Biggio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文将语言模型拒答抑制重新表述为针对线性探针的潜在空间规避攻击，并提出可控潜在空间规避方法以提升攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有通过消融模型激活中的“拒答方向”来抑制安全拒答的做法虽有效，但缺乏对其潜在空间变换机制及其为何有效的原则性解释；同时，现有方法仅将表示推到决策边界，可能不足以进入回答区域。

Method: 作者把拒答与回答提示的区分建模为线性探针问题，证明差值均值方向可自然定义探针，而沿该方向消融等价于投影到探针决策边界；在此基础上提出 Controlled Latent-space Evasion，通过将表示越过边界并优化置信度，使其进入更偏向回答的潜在区域。

Result: 该方法在15个指令微调、多模态和推理模型上取得当前最优攻击成功率，优于既有拒答消融基线和专门的越狱攻击方法。

Conclusion: 论文为拒答抑制提供了统一的潜在空间规避攻击解释，并指出仅投影到边界的局限；通过可控地越过边界可更有效地削弱拒答行为。

Abstract: Safety-aligned language models are trained to refuse harmful requests, yet refusal behavior can be suppressed by steering their internal representations. Existing methods do so by ablating a refusal direction from model activations, aiming to remove refusal from the model's residual stream. Despite their empirical success, these methods lack a principled account of the latent-space transformation they induce and why it suppresses refusal. In this work, we recast refusal suppression as a latent-space evasion attack against linear probes trained to separate refused from answered prompts. Under this view, prior work's difference-in-means direction naturally defines such a probe, and its ablation is exactly a projection onto its decision boundary, i.e., a minimum-confidence evasion attack. This perspective not only explains the empirical success of prior work but also admits a key limitation: evasion stops at the decision boundary, motivating the need to push representations further into the compliant region, i.e., where the model answers. We leverage this by proposing a Controlled Latent-space Evasion attack that projects representations past the boundary with an optimized confidence. We achieve state-of-the-art attack success rate across 15 instruction-tuned, multimodal, and reasoning models, outperforming existing refusal-ablation baselines and specialized jailbreak attacks.

</details>


### [195] [AttuneBench: A Conversation-Based Benchmark for LLM Emotional Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21739)
*Kate M. Lubrano,Faisal Sayed,Ankita Rathod,Akshansh,Craver Corbyn Thomas-Smith,Mark E. Whiting,Karina Nguyen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 AttuneBench：基于真实多轮人机对话与用户逐轮情绪/偏好标注的情绪智能评测基准，用于更直接地评估 LLM 在情绪识别、行为判断、偏好预测和回应质量方面的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有情绪智能评测多依赖合成提示、单轮案例或第三方标注，难以衡量模型在真实多轮对话中如何持续推断并回应具体用户的情绪状态与期望。随着 LLM 承担更多日常对话角色，评估其情绪智能变得重要。

Method: 作者构建了包含 200 段真实多轮人机对话的 AttuneBench。参与者与匿名 LLM 对话，并在每轮标注自身情绪状态、模型行为以及更偏好的回应。研究对 11 个模型进行评测，覆盖情绪识别、行为分类、偏好预测和回应质量判断等维度。

Result: 实验发现，不同维度上的模型排名大体相互独立，说明情绪智能行为由多个可分离能力构成。相比情绪标签准确率，偏好对齐和回应质量评判更能区分模型差异。

Conclusion: 情绪智能不仅是识别情绪标签，还需要在上下文中预测特定用户想要何种回应。单轮或合成评测难以捕捉这种跨轮动态。AttuneBench 可用于分解评估相关能力，并诊断不同模型在情绪显著对话中的优势与失败模式。

Abstract: Emotional intelligence (EI), the ability to perceive, understand, and respond appropriately to others' emotional states, is central to human communication, and increasingly important to assess as LLMs assume conversational roles in everyday life. Existing EI benchmarks rely on synthetic prompts, single-turn cases, or third-party annotation. These approaches do not directly measure how models infer and respond to a participant's emotional state over the course of a real conversation. We introduce AttuneBench, a benchmark grounded in 200 genuine multi-turn human-model conversations in which participants conversed with anonymized LLMs and provided turn-by-turn annotations of their emotional state, the model's behavior, and their preferred responses. Across 11 evaluated models, we find that model rankings on emotion recognition, behavioral classification, preference prediction, and judged response quality are largely independent, indicating that emotionally intelligent behavior decomposes into separable capabilities. Preference alignment and response-quality judgments are substantially more model-discriminating than emotion-label accuracy. These results indicate that emotionally intelligent behavior requires predicting what kind of response a specific user wants in context, a distinction that aggregate scoring can obscure and that single-turn or synthetic formats cannot directly capture across turns. AttuneBench provides a framework for assessing each of these capabilities and for diagnosing model-specific strengths and failure modes in emotionally salient conversation.

</details>


### [196] [Who Uses AI? Platforms, Workforce, and AI Exposure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21743)
*Michelle Yin,Burhan Ogut*

TL;DR: 本文指出，用AI平台对话日志衡量职业暴露度会受到平台用户群体构成的显著影响，可能偏离真实劳动力结构。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者在固定结果变量、样本、控制变量和估计器的条件下，仅改变平台输入来源，比较就业系数变化；进一步比较同一供应商的消费者端与企业端数据，并将暴露度指标按美国劳工统计局劳动力份额重新加权。同时，形式化非经典测量误差，推导就业弹性的概率极限和部分识别界限。

Result: 仅改变平台输入，ChatGPT之后就业系数变化达到1.9倍；同一供应商的消费者端与企业端渠道甚至给出符号相反的估计。按劳动力份额重新加权后，估计值衰减42%至93%。

Conclusion: 基于AI平台日志的职业暴露度指标存在非经典测量误差，容易把平台用户构成误当作劳动力暴露度。该偏误对替代效应的低估程度大于对增强效应的低估，因此相关就业影响估计需谨慎解释。

Abstract: A growing literature uses artificial intelligence platform conversation logs to measure occupation exposure. We show that these scores partly measure platform user base rather than the workforce. Holding outcome, sample, controls, and estimator fixed while varying only the platform input changes the post-ChatGPT employment coefficient by a factor of 1.9, and within-vendor consumer-versus-enterprise channels produce estimates that disagree in sign. Reweighting to Bureau of Labor Statistics workforce shares attenuates estimates by 42 to 93 percent. We formalize the non-classical measurement error, derive probability limits and partial-identification bounds for employment elasticities. The bias understates substitution more than augmentation.

*Henry Salgado,Meagan R. Kendall,Martine Ceberio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合因果发现与基于论证推理的可解释AI方法，用于解释模型为何可能做出某类预测。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有XAI方法通常能指出哪些特征与预测相关，但难以说明模型为何做出特定决策；因此需要一种能表达因果关系及支持/反对理由的解释框架。

Method: 方法先使用因果发现识别变量间的因果关系，再将这些关系转化为双极论证框架（BAF），表示特征之间的支持与攻击交互；随后基于半稳定语义寻找可解释特定输出的特征扩展集合。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将因果建模与论证框架结合有助于弥补传统XAI只关注相关特征的不足，为模型预测提供结构化、可推理的解释。

Abstract: Explainable AI (XAI) methods identify which features are relevant to a model's predictions but often fail to clarify why certain decisions are made. In this work, we present a novel method that integrates causality with argument-based reasoning to explain why models may be making predictions. Our approach first identifies causal relationships among variables using causal discovery methods and then translates these into a Bipolar Argumentation Framework (BAF) to represent supportive and opposing interactions among features. By using semi-stable semantics, we find extensions of features that explain why certain outcomes may have been chosen. We demonstrate our method on two benchmark datasets and compare its results against standard post-hoc explainability approaches.
